'%anglais%' UNION SELECT * FROM users where experience LIKE '%anglais%' UNION SELECT * FROM users where nomprojet LIKE '%anglais%' UNION SELECT * FROM users where origine LIKE '%anglais%' UNION SELECT * FROM users where langues LIKE '%anglais%' UNION SELECT * FROM users where langues2 LIKE '%anglais%' UNION SELECT * FROM users where langues3 LIKE '%anglais%' UNION SELECT * FROM users where langues4 LIKE '%anglais%' UNION SELECT * FROM users where languesniveau LIKE '%anglais%' UNION SELECT * FROM users where languesniveau2 LIKE '%anglais%' UNION SELECT * FROM users where languesniveau3 LIKE '%anglais%' UNION SELECT * FROM users where languesniveau4 LIKE '%anglais%'  order by nom  LIMIT 10 OFFSET 0; ----

'%bilingue%'  AND sexe = 'F' UNION SELECT * FROM users where tranche LIKE '%bilingue%'  AND sexe = 'F' UNION SELECT * FROM users where taille LIKE '%bilingue%'  AND sexe = 'F' UNION SELECT * FROM users where cheveux LIKE '%bilingue%'  AND sexe = 'F' UNION SELECT * FROM users where cp LIKE '%bilingue%'  AND sexe = 'F' UNION SELECT * FROM users where sexe LIKE '%bilingue%'  AND sexe = 'F' UNION SELECT * FROM users where taille LIKE '%bilingue%'  AND sexe = 'F' UNION SELECT * FROM users where telephone LIKE '%bilingue%'  AND sexe = 'F' UNION SELECT * FROM users where departement LIKE '%bilingue%'  AND sexe = 'F' UNION SELECT * FROM users where poids LIKE '%bilingue%'  AND sexe = 'F' UNION SELECT * FROM users where yeux LIKE '%bilingue%'  AND sexe = 'F' UNION SELECT * FROM users where signesparticulier LIKE '%bilingue%'  AND sexe = 'F' UNION SELECT * FROM users where danse1 LIKE '%bilingue%'  AND sexe = 'F' UNION SELECT * FROM users where danse2 LIKE '%bilingue%'  AND sexe = 'F' UNION SELECT * FROM users where danse3 LIKE '%bilingue%'  AND sexe = 'F' UNION SELECT * FROM users where discipline1 LIKE '%bilingue%'  AND sexe = 'F' UNION SELECT * FROM users where discipline2 LIKE '%bilingue%'  AND sexe = 'F' UNION SELECT * FROM users where discipline3 LIKE '%bilingue%'  AND sexe = 'F' UNION SELECT * FROM users where langues LIKE '%bilingue%'  AND sexe = 'F' UNION SELECT * FROM users where langues2 LIKE '%bilingue%'  AND sexe = 'F' UNION SELECT * FROM users where langues3 LIKE '%bilingue%'  AND sexe = 'F' UNION SELECT * FROM users where rolerecherche LIKE '%bilingue%'  AND sexe = 'F' UNION SELECT * FROM users where experience LIKE '%bilingue%'  AND sexe = 'F' UNION SELECT * FROM users where nomprojet LIKE '%bilingue%'  AND sexe = 'F' UNION SELECT * FROM users where origine LIKE '%bilingue%'  AND sexe = 'F' UNION SELECT * FROM users where langues LIKE '%bilingue%'  AND sexe = 'F' UNION SELECT * FROM users where langues2 LIKE '%bilingue%'  AND sexe = 'F' UNION SELECT * FROM users where langues3 LIKE '%bilingue%'  AND sexe = 'F' UNION SELECT * FROM users where langues4 LIKE '%bilingue%'  AND sexe = 'F' UNION SELECT * FROM users where languesniveau LIKE '%bilingue%'  AND sexe = 'F' UNION SELECT * FROM users where languesniveau2 LIKE '%bilingue%'  AND sexe = 'F' UNION SELECT * FROM users where languesniveau3 LIKE '%bilingue%'  AND sexe = 'F' UNION SELECT * FROM users where languesniveau4 LIKE '%bilingue%'  AND sexe = 'F'  AND sexe = 'F'   LIMIT 10 OFFSET 10; ----
